RESUME OF CHANGES APPLIED (PATCH 5 BASELINE)

1) HierarchyFactory forwarding (UTP-safe)
    - Keep `IConnectionListener` on `HierarchyFactory`.
    - Forward `OnConnected(conn, asServer)` and `OnDisconnected(conn, asServer)` to all `HierarchyV2` instances.
    - Keep catchup trace logs in factory to confirm callback path is executed.

2) Server catchup dedupe + robust trigger in HierarchyV2
    - Add `_pendingServerCatchupConnections` and `_serverCatchupDone`.
    - In `OnConnected`: if player already resolvable => `TryServerCatchup(playerId)`, else queue connection in pending.
    - In `OnServerPostPlayerJoined`: resolve/remove pending connection and call `TryServerCatchup(playerId)`.
    - In `TryServerCatchup`: prevent duplicate runs with `_serverCatchupDone.Add(playerId)` guard.
    - Keep host bridge: `OnPlayerReceivedID` calls `other.TryServerCatchup(player)`.

3) Catchup deferred spawn handling
    - In `CatchupClient`, when identity is in `_toSpawnNextFrame`, do NOT just skip:
      - call `TryAddObserver(playerId)`
      - invoke `onObserverAdded`
      - invoke `TriggerOnPreObserverAdded`
      - enqueue `_triggerLateObserverAdded`
    - Track and log `deferredToNormalSpawn` in catchup trace.

4) Immediate visibility fallback after catchup
    - Keep `EvaluateVisibilityForPlayer(playerId)` after `CatchupClient(playerId)` in `TryServerCatchup`.

CURRENT LOG RESULT (new logs)
    - Catchup path executes and dedupe works.
    - Remaining failure pattern: second join still shows deferred identities, e.g.
      `CatchupClient finished ... sentSpawnEvents=42 deferredToNormalSpawn=14 spawnedIdentities=56`.

NEXT FIX TO APPLY
    - Add a second visibility pass AFTER deferred spawns are finalized:
      a) Add `HashSet<PlayerID> _playersNeedingDeferredVisibilityPass` in `HierarchyV2`.
      b) In `CatchupClient`, if `deferredCount > 0`, add `playerId` to this set.
      c) In `SpawnDelayedIdentities`, after processing delayed identities, call
          `EvaluateVisibilityForPlayer(player)` for each queued player, then clear the set.

EXPECTED VALIDATION
    - Keep seeing: `TryServerCatchup executing`, `TryServerCatchup skipped duplicate`.
    - On second join, `deferredToNormalSpawn` may still be >0 initially, but missing objects should no longer persist after deferred finalize tick.
